You HAVE to add the cheese, if you go with somebody who is lactose intolerant, don't go with them. You must add the cheese, it's incredible. < text>
Great food okay price . Place is very small so order out and enjoy at home. The service might seem unfriendly to none Koreans. But they're  old school Koreans so no small talk don't get offended.  Customer services means get your food as quick as possible and maybe a smile. They might have a distressed look on there face while taking your order but trust me it isn't you they're stressing on something else. Food is AWESOME . Rice and side orders complimentary with most soups.  And the Kim chee is on point. I've only had soups but there noodles look good I'm gonna try it this week . FYI :  before you leave grab a menu so you can order on the phone next time and have it ready when you get there.< /text>

< review>
The Sul Lang Tang Soup was just what i needed as i was feeling body aches, chills and an onset of a fever.

This is my new go-to Sul Lang Tang place. The broth is delicious: milky-color flavored with the bones that have been stewing for hours. the service is great! They also give a variety of banchan.

I don't want to share this gem because i don't want there to be a wait the next time i go -- but i do wish for others to know how good the food tastes here.

There is a parking lot but often times -- it is crowded. Thank goodness it is not LA and there is ample parking on the street as well.</review>

<user_name>KELLY SABROE</user_name><gmapID>0x80945f2c8699c4df:0xe1cb783519012088</gmapID>< text>
Delicious donuts with a smile! One of the local gems of the Sunnyside neighborhood. The owners are hardworking, kind, attentive, give back to the local community & really get to know their regular customers.
They serve all of the regular types of donuts one would expect, plus a few specialty items of their own too, such as beerocks. They're also one of the few places in town who make Giant Cinnamon Rolls (in the Country Fair Style) and they're just fabulous! A family favorite of ours. It's very obvious the owners take pride in what they make.
Bottom Line: They make great food at a reasonable price with excellent service!< /text>

My husband and I were staying across the street at the Marriott & he sent me to go get a mixed burrito. When I told the cashier what I wanted, he went to the kitchen & asked the cook to come talk to me. The cook told me mixed burritos aren't on their menu because they didn't have shredded beef but that he would be happy to make a special mixed burrito however I wanted it. I told him to surprise me. It was delicious! He made it with carne asada meat, cheese, beans, rice, sour cream, guacamole & green sauce. Even better than the food was the super nice, friendly cook who provided me with awesome customer service which showed me that he values & appreciates their customers.< /text>

<text>I read about this place yesterday in Eater SF, as it just opened a month ago, and had to check it out same day. The article talked about the artisnal cocktails, lobster rolls (or bites) and a venue that was 'dripping in plants'. The article was spot on. You walk into an initiate space with soft colors, vaulted ceilings and plants up above surrounding the space. The service was quite charming and the food was incredible. The menu is relatively limited with what appears to be a focus on quality over quantity. We ordered the chicken tenders (aka chicken 'tendies'), slider, fries and the ever-so-decadent lobster roll.
